/bram ze bsod kyang stobs bzhi yongs su tshang gyur pa s/
/gnyen po kun spyod sngags idan 'di la 'bad pa na/
/sgrib pa'i phung po ma lus 'dag la sol snyi ci/

ru ka'i lha khang du logs bris su bzhugs pa dạng/ de bzhin ras

ff. 20
Manuscript belonging to A-pho Rin-po-che.
.
/bla ma rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/
slob dpon klu sgrub kyi zhal nas/
7gang gis ma rtogs pa yis rtogs pa'i spyod pa mi bya ste/
/byas na rgyal po'i khrims la dmangs kyis gnod pa byas pa bzhin/
Zrtogs pa mnams kyis ma rtogs pa yi spyod pa mi bya ste
/byas na glang chen dag ni dam du bying ba 'dra gsung ngo/
slob dpon sa ra ha'i zhal nas/
kye 'o grogs dag lhan cig skyes pa ste/
Zgzhan nas mnyed min zhal la dris/
don dam gzhan gyi ngo bo de rtogs na/
7yid ni gar 'ching rlung yang chad pa med gsung ngo/
slob dpon tog tse pa'i zhal nas/
7tha mal shes pa snying, gi dbus su sad/
tshogs drug dag (f. lv) na bde chen rgyun mi 'chad/
Zbrtags pa thams cad don med g.yeng ba'i rgyu/
sgom du med pas gnyug ma'i ngang la zhog gsung ngo/
slob dpon sa man ta badzra'i zhal nas/
Zphyag rgya chen po rang la lhun gyis grub pa ste/
mi bsam mi rig 'bad pa med pa rang gis zhog/
chad pa med de sngon du nyams nyong rang gis rig/
/rtag par mi gyur mngon zhen med par zung du 'jug gsung ngo/
slob dpon ka na pa'i zhal nas/
shing rta'i 'khor lo gcig dang mi ldan 'gro bar mi nus bzhin/
7sbyin sogs 'bad pa byas kyang bla ma'i man ngag med na dngos grub
dam pa med/
/bya rgod rtsal (f. 2r) rdzogs 'dab mar bcas pa dag ni mkha' la
spyod cing rgyug/
/skal bzang rnal 'byor dam pa rnams ni dbang dang byin brlabs dam
pa'i 'og tu chud cing bde gsung ngo/
kampa la'i zhal nas/
zab cing rgya che rgya mtsho nor bus gang ba la/
klu yi rgyal po rnams kyi mnga' mdzod ngo mtshar che/
snang grags thams cad ye nas chos sku yin pa la/
/rtogs dang nyams smyong idan pas mnga mdzod ngo mtshar che gsung ngo/
slob dpon lū yi pa'i zhal nas/
khyi rgod rab tu mi srun sna la sbrang rtsi byugs na phyogs rnams
kun tu za bar byed/
/blo aman skal pa dman pa'i gang zag mnams la dbang dang gdams ngag
byin pas rang rgyud bsreg/
/glang chen dpa' la brtan pa'i sna la ral gri bskur bas dgra dpung
'joms/
/skal bzang (f. 2v) blo ldan skye med rtogs pa mnams kyis thug phrad
dag gi mam rtog 'joms gsungo/
slob dpon te lo pa'i zhal nas/
/ri rab gser gyi ngos la bya gnas pa/
bya yi rang bzhin bor nas gser du snang,
/mkhas pa gang gis skye ba med rtogs na
angos po'i rang bzhin bor nas bde ba che gsung ngo/
/tai lo pa'i zhal nas/

On the 'cham: Bla ma dgongs 'dus
Bla ma dgongs pa 'dus pa las: Gar "cham gyi lag len phrul gyi
pa tra. From volume 3 Ga) of an eastern Tibetan print of the
Bla ma dgongs 'dus collection.

-
na mo ghu ru dhe wa dā kki ni hüm:
ye shes rol pa dbang gi dkyil 'khor du:
zhi rgyas la sogs bang mdzod dgos 'dod 'byung:
gar dgu'i nyams ldan dpal chen he ru ka:
sprul pa du ma gyed pa khyed phyag 'tshal:
khro rgyal 'bar ba'i klong las rang byung ba:
gang la gang 'dul bzhed pa'i rnam
syur can:
mos blos gdul bya'i dbang tshul ci bzhin ltar:
phyi nang gsang gsum gar 'cham gtan la abab:
di la sngon 'gro dngos gzhi rjes gsum las:
thog mar sngon du 'gro ba'i rim pa ni:
phyi nang (f. lv) gsang gsum gar 'cham chas gos mams:
gang lag, la dgos phyag mtshan rgyan cha sogs:
mkho ba'i yo byad gzhung ltar sta gon bya:
gang du byed pa'i sa phyogs go dogs bsal:
yul ris gzhi bdag bka' bsgo gser skyems btang:
bden pa'i stobs briod mched 1cam tha dag tshogs: or: brngod
gral la 'khod dam gar 'dug skabs dang bstun:
gtso 'khor rkang grangs inga dgu bcu gcig gam:
bcu gsum
am ni nyer bdun la sogs pa:
gang yod 'di ltar chas dang dan par bya:
de yang cha lugs phyi nang (f. 2r) gsang gsum ste:
phyi Itar phod ka g.yang lug lhab lhub gos:
mun tsa cod pan dar 'phyang thor cog dang:
khro 'bag mgo brnyan gdong zhal zhi dang khro:
gnas skabs tshul dang bstun pas gang rigs 8.yogs:
me tog thod bcings dbu rgyan srog zhu spras:
mdzes shing lhun chags gzi brjid ldan par bya:
phyag ntshan bhan phur gri thod gang rigs las:
os pa'i rgyan gyis 'chams par brgyan la 'cham: read: 'tshams
mnga stabs bstun phyir rnga 'dzin cha lugs kyang:
brjid pa'i thod dang srid pa'i spyi lugs zhwa:
phyi ru lding ber ma mo'i ral pa dang:
the'u rkyang ba dan g.yab pa'i gos dang bcas:
phan tshun stabs bstun rigs pas gtan la phab:
mnga stabs gcig nas bzung ste dgu yi bar:
gyur brdungs grangs brdungs 'thed brdungs la sogs kyang:
bar mtshams gar byed rol mo'i sba dang bcas:
skad kyi gdangs dang phyag rgyali so mtshams bsgyur:
ram gyur stabs kyi rol mo'i brdungs stabs bsgyur:
gnyis ka'i stangs kyis thabs shes cham stabs rams:
rnam 'gyur gang byed gcig la gcig ltos te:
kun (f. 2v) kyang lus ngag yid kyi rtsa bzhi Itod:
phan tshun zur gyis 'tsho zhing 'grigs par 'cham:
hūm ring hüm thung sngags sgra sgrogs bya zhing:
dang po
cham tshul shin tu dal bar bya:
bar du lus dal nang du shes pa bsgrim:
jog med par gnyis mnyam gtan la phab:
tha ma drag shul yang rtsal gang yod phyung:
yem yem tsan tsan bar snang lding tshul bya:
pho nya myur mgyogs skyi 'dong dbab dang mtshungs:
gsang bar g.yang gzhi ko rlon stag sham dang:
gcer bu'i lus la thal chen tshon gyis byugs:
ngo shun gang 'thad so so'i skabs dang bstun:

Incipit:
Ina mo manydzu gho şā ya/ 'chi med bdag po'i gtsug gis nor
bus zhabs mthil 'khor lo rtag tu bsten pas mtha' dag dreg pa cig
car zlog/ rang rang mos pa dang mthun sna tshogs sku yi zlos gar
srid pa gsum gyi khyon rams ma lus yongs su 'gengs/ gang sku
mthong ba'i mod la dang bas drangs pa'i dga' bdag gzhal med gzhan
las phul byung sbyin mdzad dam pa'i skyes/ zla med gyur pa grags
snyan 'od kyi phyogs mams mo'i ma rgyan mdzes by ed zas gtsang
sras kyi zhabs la "dud/
mkhyen pa yangs pas shes bya'i gnas kun cig car mjal/
brtse ba'i 'od (f. lv) kyi mtha' yas 'gro la thugs rje'i sprin/
nus pas char rgyun mam par spro bas sdug bsngal gyis/
gdung ba ma lus sel mdzad 'jam dpal dbyangs la 'dud/
rgyal ba ma lus sna tshogs snang ba'i sku
sems can mos pa ji bzhin ston pa'i phyir/
nor gyi gdungs la nor skyong skur ston pa'i/
nor lha'i tshogs kyi 'gro 'di bsrung gyur cig/
mthar thug don la bzang ngan ma grub kyang/
snang tshul ci ru (= tsam du) cir yang char bas na/
'jig rten lugs kyi bstan bcos rjes 'brengs te/
tha snyad bden pa ji bzhin bshad par bya] (f. 2r)
Manuscript seen through Kunsang Topgay of Bhutan.

Bzo rig works
Shakabpa reports (June 1972) that he has seen a manuscript lacking
the first title folio on bzo-rig:
/dbu shog ma tshang ba abu med kyi bris pa sku gsung
thugs rten/ rol mo (ris mo?)/ gos chen/ akar yoi/ khrab
mams/ gri rta sga sogs brtag dpyad byed tshui/ me
spre 1o/ bkra shis rnam rgyal gyis padma bkod pa'i
chos sder bris pa shog grangs 73 yod pa zhig 'dug/
Joseph F. Weiler
41, Hillcrest Terrace
Meriden, Connecticut, 06450
-
This work is obviously the Nor dpyad rgya mtsho of Bya 'Jam-
-dbyangs Bkra-shis-ram-rgyal, a student of the 7th Zhwa-nag
Karma-pa Choş-grags-rgya-mtsho. The work must have been written
in about 1536 or possibly 1476.



o not

Roerich, p. viii
"Another historical work qyoted by 'Gos lo-tsā-ba is the chos-'byuri
or "History of Buddhism" by Nel-pa pandita Grags-pa sMon-lam tshul-
-khrims, known by the abbreviated title of Nel-pa'i chos-'byuri. This
chos-' byuri is based on a somewhat different historical tradition, and
its chronology merits a closer study".
M
Roerich quotes with the full name on p. 61 (f. 27b/28r)
We can date him to the early 19th century from p. 750-751 where only
Nel-pa Pan-chen is given:
Mkhas-grub Chos-rje (d. 1319)'s disciple Gser-gling-pa Bkra-
-shis-dpal (1792–1365) Växx received final monastic ordination from
Nel-pa Pan-chen and studied the Vinaya, Abhidharma, Prajnaparamita,
and logic with Nel-pa khu-dbon at Gsang-phu

brgya skor bcas rgyu nor ita ba mig gis mi bzod/ bsam pa sems
kyis mi langs pa yod pa'i zhang zhung rgyal po'i tshong pa nag
po rgya la "gro mi zer te stag rong gi sa thog tu sgar babs nas
yod pa stag rong đpon gyog gnyis kyis rig ste) a khu khro thung
gis de bcom dgos snyam nas nyo tshong cung zad byas te phyir
log nas a khu'i sras lha rgod spun gnyis la ya gi'i tshong zog
rgya chen 'dug pas bcom dgos tshul gsungs pas/ gzhan ma blon
tshogs mams sems la ma song rung/ kho'i dbang du song ba'i
phyir nam skya rengs shar ba dang mnyam du/ sras lha rgod spun
myis dang zhang ne nyi ma rang shar a khu beas rta amag nội
shu sgar du mchongs nas/ rgyu nor rta drel bcas gnang du bcad/
mi mams gcig kyang (p. i) med par bsad/
Terminatur:
/zhang gling g.yul 'gyed dpa' bo dgyes pa'i dga' ston dang
skyid pa'i glu dbyangs 'di phyi rabs ma ba'i bcud du 'bru nyung
don bsdus la rgyas pa'i don tshang bar lhag bsam mam dag gi
yi ger btab pas/ bdud rigs nag phyogs thams cad (p. 147) ming
med du zhi nas akar po'i chos kyi bstan sa dar rgyas yun brtan
gong 'phel du byung bar si ddi bandza yan tu/ sa wa mang ga lam/
bkra shis dpal bar "dzam gling rgyas gyur cig/ dzam gling khyon
la ble skyiả 'byung bar shog/

Tibetan historical works

bya ba bzhugs 80.

ff. 224
Missing: ff. 35-39
From Lahul: seen through Khesdrup Gyatso Shashin, October 1976
Incipit:
om ma pi pad me hüm/ (f. lv)
phags pa thugs rje'i bdag po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la
phyag tshal lo/
/gro (f. 2r) ba'i re skong dgos 'dod 'byung ba'i dpal/
Zrkang gnyis gtso bo yon tan kun gyi gter/
Iha mi'i ston pa shākya'i rgyal po la/
Alus ngag yid gsum gus pas phyag 'tshaí 1o/
Atshad med mkhyen rtse'i thugs rje rab rgyas pas/ (f. 20)
gang la gang dul sprul pa bod yul gyi
gro rnams smin groi lam la 'god mdzad pa/
spyan ras gzigs dbang de la phyag 'tshai 10/
Zapag med bsod nams lhun grub mi'i dbang/
mang pos skur ba'i gdung rgyud rin po che/
bu ram shing pa la sogs rgya (f. 3r) gar gyi/
rnam dag rgyal rgyud mams la phyag 'Tshal 10/

dam pa'i chos kyis sgron me chen po spar
bod bangs sems can bde la 'god mdzad pa' i!
sprul pa'i rgyal blon rams la phyag 'tshal lo/

Tshe-ring-dbang-rgyal
389
pas yi ge 'dri ba dang/ rdel rtsis kyi dpe cha 'dzin skyong sogs
tshang ma'i slob dpon 'khur du bzhes te bslab bya mdzad pa yang
gus shing dang ba dang bcas mthar phyin pa gsan/
gzhung sa'i bla rtsis pa khro rgyal dpal mgon dang/ smin grol
gling nas dge slong blo gsal ram gnyis nas snyan ngag me long
le'u gnyis pa tshar re khrid par rjes po sa lta bu las bka' tshegs
med par thugs su chud pas rtsom rgyugs kyang phul grub cing/ dge
slong blo gsal nas/
'jigs med grags pa'i legs bshad yongs 'du'i tshal/
Alas 'ongs bstod tshig utpa la gzhon nu'i phreng/
abyangs can dga' ba tshe ring dbang rgyal gyi/
/rnam đpyod mgul ba'i rgyan du bdag gis spel/ /zhes rig gnas kyi
mtshan gsol dang/ bsngags brjod mang du mdzad/
'di dag gi skabs su byang stag lung gi gdan sa'i khri la bzhugs
dgos zhes gra gling sogs 'dus tshogs phal cher nas don gnyer chen
pos zhus 'dug kyang/ gdung rabs nyag phra ba dang/ gzhung sa'i zhabs
'degs sogs mdzad dgos



kyi stabs na 'grig/ de rjes nag chur yab rje dang mnyam du yod
thog/ gong sa rgyal dbang mchog nas zhabs gras su dgos tshul phebs
kyang re zhig dgongs zhu mdzad/
lcag yos dgung lo bco inga pa'i thog (1711) nas brtsam smin
gling du nges pa don gyi mkhas pa'i mchog lo chen dharma shri'i
zhabs pad bsnyen te snyan ngag me long le'u gsum ka skar rtsis
kyi ri mo yongs rdzogs/ lan war sogs yig rigs bcas pa'i na pa'i
mus lal chab mdo rgyal ba 'phags pa lha sku bsnyun bag gi bcos
thabs la/ lo chen rin po che gdan zhus mdzad pa'i re zhig 'phro
can du lus kyang/ chu sbrul lo (1713) slar yang/ sgra dbyangs can
ma yongs rdzogs/ sdebs sbyor rin chen 'byung ldan/ skar rtsis kyi
phro sogs lo chen sku dngos kyi ljags khrid gnang ba'i sgra'i
ri mo yongs rdzogs grub nas/ tshangs sras dgyes pa'i blo idan zhes
mtshan kyang gsol/
slob dpon thugs yid 'dres pa'i rjesu bzung zhing zhabs
'dis chos zhig mdzad na bstan 'gror phan bzhes dang yang gsungs/



Tshe-ring-dbang-rgyala 3
anos
390
lo snga phyir slob gnyer mdzad skabs/ ljags bshad nyan pa
sogs don yod nges ma gtogs spro seng sogs bag yangs gtan nas mi mdzad
pa'i bzhugs gnas kyi sgo'i them pa 'da' ma myong ba sogs thugs rus
brtson 'grus shin tu che ba'i stabs/ dbu skra lan gcig 'khru ba'i
skabs lan tshar gri chu gi shag dgos sogs byung ba'i sku yon la
brtson te snying rus che ba dang/ mkhyen rabs kyi 'jug sgo shin tu
yangs pa'i nges pa don gyi pandi ta chen po rigs pa'i gnas Inga
thogs med na smra ba'i sengge lta bur gyur/
di skabs gter chen chos kyi rgyal po 'gyur med rdo rje yang
yang mjal phrad mdzad cing phyag phul ba na stan las bzhengs pa
dang dbu sdug mdzad pa sogs mthong sos shin tu che/ bkal las kyang
rigs kyi bu la rgyud kyi lha 'go zhes/ khyed rang bod kyi mi drag
tsho da Ita nas yon tan la brtson pa bskyes dgos tshul sogs bka'
slob don gyi snying po can mang du stsal/ gter gsar rig 'dzin thugs
tig dang tshe dbang gur drag rta mgrin sogs kyi dbang rjes gnang
kyang mang du gsan/
gdung sras padma 'gyur med rgya mtsho las 'jigs by ed lha bcu
gsum ma'i dbang chen gsan



te 'di nas brtsams re lhag pa'i lha mchog du bsny en cing sgrabled
gter chen chos kyi rgyal po gdul bya rtag 'dzin can gyi ngor rig
'dzin mkha' gro'i gnas su gshegs pa'i tshe yang namkha' nas rol mo'i
sgra dang dri zhim po'i dus pa 'thul/ 'ja' sprin sogs ngo mtshar
ba'i bkod pa du ma gzigs shing gdung mjal thog smon lam mtha' yas
pa'i mtshams sbyor mdzad/ de nas mi ring bar yab rje'i drung du
lha ldan du phebs nas rgyal po lha sang gi bkalung bsgyur ba'i
skabs yin par mjal phyag dang bcas srid chen po'i drung na spyod
pa'i gras su thog mar snyan ngag gi rtsom rgyug chos brjod gsum
sgrigs du sbyar ba sogs phul ba'i dgyes pa chen pos gnang cha
stsal/
shing rta lo (1714) grub dbang rin po che ngag dbang bstan
dzin dpal 'byor bzang po ndo mkhar du spyan drangs/ chos dang
zang zing gi 'brel bas thugs tshim shing/ nyid nas tshig don
bzang po'i nyams mgur gyi mchod sprin spro ba yang gang/
shing lug 10 (1715) mdo mkhar ba'i sras dang rje nyid thun
mong la ja khri dpon gyi sras mo mam rgyal dbang mo mthun
jug
tu khab bzhes mdzad kyang mi ring bar tha dad
.



Tshe-ring-dbang-rgyal
391
du gyur/
dgung lo nyi shu pa me sprel lor (1716) bzhis ka bsam 'grub
rtse'i bca' khral 'bab yongs bsdu bar bkas mngags pa bzhin phebs/
pan chen thans cad mkhyen gzigs la mjal phyag mdzad cing/ rdzogs
dpon sogs ri şi'i chab zhugs spro seng dang 'grig pa'i der phebs
nas/ srid sgrub kyi khengs pa 'phrog pa'i nyag phran gyi rtsed 'jo
gzhan dag spobs pa zhur ba byas bca khral bsdu len sogs gang gi
thad la yang chos rgyal dge abang dang/ pha las nu'i mam thar
bzhin grangs 'bo gtan la phab pa las deng sang gi skye bo tha shal

pa'i 'bangs mams ril ltar btser ba'i ngan mjog mkhan gyi mam thar

bzhin par/ bzhis rtser rdzogs chen du rtsis dpon lum pa gnas dang/

jus rams shor/ sbyong dgar ba'i mong khams la dbang bsgyur ba'i

'dzin sde srid kyi khri la mnga" gsol/ bod kyi mi drag dang bla

sogs yo langs shin tu che/
lo chen rda rma shri yang skyi chu'i gram du dkrong rtsis byas

Taranatha
392
dgos pa sogs rta bsig che zhing sku ngal gnang ltar/ tshad las 'das
pa byung ba dang/ bla ma 'khru nas dang zhabs drung nyid bzung
nas gzhung gi sku rim mnan gtad kyi bkod pa byas zhes nyin cig yongs
bzhes khang du sgom skyil byung yang mtha' sgrol phug pa dang non
'khyung byung zhes sgor skyil bya mi sogs po'i lags nas rta sga byir
re sprod yin bden bsrol dang bcas sku nyid la nyes skyon du ma
gyur/
pan chen rin po cher sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i rjes gnang
kyang gsan/ gzhis rtse las dgongs khrol zhus pas lcag rtse gri
gu rdzongs dpon gyi 'khur 'dzin du bzhugs/
stag rtse sde srid nas bsam yas mdo sde mchod pa'i skabs
grems rgyu'i gos thang bzheng bar legs 'bul gya nom stsal/ rab
ston gyi tshe skye bo rgyu rtsal gyi bsnyen pa du ma'i dbus su
'tshad ragi rtsed 'jor zhugs pas sku lus kyi skyoms 'gyur gzhan las
khyad par du thon pa dang/ chibs rgyug gi rtsa ba bzang shos kyi
bsngags brjod dar dir sgrog pa byung/
rgyal sras rin po che las rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi mngon rtogs
bklags chog ma'i ljags lugs kyang gsan/ lha ldan
1



du yab rje tshangs pa chen po sku nyams med bde bar gyur nas lha
sras zhabs drung nyi nas stag rtse sde srid kyi mgron gnyer dang/
drung yig gnyis cog thugs 'khur bzhes/
1cags byi lo (1720) stag rtse sdesrid nas bsam yas kyi jo bo
byang chub chen po'i dbu rgyan snyan rgyan ngun rgyan sogs rin po
che du ma'i phra tshom can bzhengs par rab gnas skabs yon bdag la
sde srid kyang tshim bsgyur gnang/ gong ma chen po'i dpung gi
bsngags pa'i rgya sog gi grangs kyi mi lang ba dang bcas/
gong sa lha mi'i gtsug rgyan rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen
gzigs chen po bdun pa bskal bzang rgya mtsho sku 'bum byams pa
gling du spyan drangs te rim gyis gshegs pa'i snyan grags la brten
sbyong gar ba'i dpung mams gong ma'i dpung gi gzi byin ma bzod
par rang gnas su ldog/ srid bzhi'i mam 'dren chen mo yan lag
bzhi'i dpung gis bsker te gru 'dzin gyi pho brang chen po'i
khri la zhabs sor bkod pa'i dga' ston ntha' yas pa spyod skabs sku
nyid mgron gnyer gyi khri nas skyongs bzhin pa yin/
de nas mi ring bar stag rtse sde srid rang bzhin bzang
zhing thugs



Lhasa and its history
Gur-bkra Chos 'byung, v. 2, ff. 553r et ff.
//zangs dkar 'phags pa shes rab ni mnga' ris zangs dkar
du 'khrungs/ lha sa'i sprang tshad bton/ lha sa bsam yas dang
mtha'
dul phal cher ste gtsug lag khang bco lnga tsam zhig
gso phul phyên mdzad/ lo toa ba chen po 'đỉ dang moi chung
bgkor dpon gnyis kyis lha sa'i jo khang bdag med du song nas
sprang tshad bcas yod pa la/ sprang po mams la khang pa dang
nor byin nas bskrad/ ma song ba mams ston mo rab sdus shul
dmag gis bzung nas bton te lha sa'i gtsug lag khang la zhabs
tog byed pa 'di las snga ma byung ste/ mdol chung bskor dpon
gyis lus ril por mar me phul skad/ de yang thang yig chen mo
las/
skabs 'ga' sprang po'i sprang tshad bcad nas bzung/
1ha'i phyag la sprad (1. 553r) pos zo ba 'dogs/
chos la sprang sprug shog 'bag byed pa 'byung/ /zhes
pa'i skabs der mchis/
lo tsa ba 'dis zhabs tog phul ba nas bzung/ de rjes dwags
po sgom tshul gyis rba 'bring gi 'khrug pas jo bor mchod pa chad
pa gsos/ rba rag dang 'bring tsho'i 'khrugs pa bsdums nas bar
skor gyi 'khor sa brtsigs jo bo gtsang khad lhor bzhugs pa
gtsang khang dbus mar gdan drangs pa zhal bsgyur ba yin yang
zer/ zhabs tog rgya cher mdzad nas zhang rin po che la gtad/
zhang rin po che dang tshal pa khri đpon rim gyis kyang zhabs
tog phul zhing/ phyi'i rag brtsigs pa yang thog mar mnga' bdag
nyang gi sras 'gro ba'i mgon po'i rdo mnams rdzu 'phrul gyis
dad nas chu rag mdzad de nas lha rje dge ba 'bum dang/ de'i
1cam ye shes mchog dang zhig po bdud rtsi sogs kyis chu rag gi
zhabs tog rgya cher mdzad/
ya tse'i rgyal po re'u smal gyis gser zangs kyi dbu gdug
dang ya tse rgyal po punye smal gyis gser tog chen mo phul
zhing/ de nas dung ntsho ras pa/ grub thob ngon yes dang/ karma
pa de bzhin gshegs pa sogs bgrangs pa las 'das shing phyis su
rje rin po che tsong kha pas longs skur zhal bsgyur (1. 553v)
zhing zhabs tog phun sum tshogs pa mazad de/ de phyin bstan 'azin
gyi skyes chen du ma dang/ 'byor Idan gyi sbyin bdag du mas bsnyen

Tsi'u-dmar-po
Gnod sbyin Tsitta dmar po'i snying gi rgyud le'u bdun pa bzhugs
SO
Marked: Bu
ff. 56 Dbu-med manuscript from the Dpal-yul group in Mysore
Contents:
1) Title work
ff. lv-5v
Incipit: Rgya gar skad du: Yak sha ra tsa siddhi: ghri ba tsitta
tantra: Bod skad du: Gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po spu gri dmar po
snying gi rgyud:
a) Gl eng gzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o
b) Skye rgyud bstan pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o
c) Rdzas dang bca' gzhi bstan pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o
a) Sngags kyi le'u ste bzhi pa'o
e) Bsnyen bsgrub rtags dang rim pa bstan pa'i le'u ste Inga pa'o
f) Blta spyod gnad kyi le'u ste drug pa'o
g) Gtad pa'i le'u ste bdun palo
Terminatur: Gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po Btsi dmar gyi rgyud Btsan
rol pa skya bdun gyi rtog pa rdzogs so: sya mya ya: rgya rgya
rgya: rje btsun mnga' ris pan chen gyis gter nas spyan drangs
pa'o:...
2) Tsitta dmar po phyi nang gsang ba yang gsang gi rten bca'
thabs bzhugs so
ff. 5v-7v
Incipit: Dpal rta mgrin la phyag 'tshal lo: gnod sbyin rol pa
skya bdun gyis rang gi srog snying mdongs gsol du phul te:
phyi gsol kha la rten nas dam can sprin ltar 'du ba dang: nang
spa lcags la rten nas dam can khyi ltar 'breng ba dang: gsang
ba bla rdo la rten nas dam can phru ltar chags pa: de kho na
nyid mdung zhags dmar po la rten nas dgra bgegs cham la 'bebs
pa dang: shog dril bzhi yod pa ni: zab mo snying gi dum bu'o:
Terminatur: Mnga' ris pan chen padma ye shes rol pa rtsal
gyis gter nas spyan drangs palo: rdo rje'i btsan pod kyi gros:
3) Tsitta dmar po'i bskul dang lo rgyus bzhugs so
ff. 71-10r
Incipit: Nyi ma nub phyogs pha gi na: btsan yul zangs thang
dmar po na: zangs brag gnam du zangs po zang:
Terminatur: Sgrub thabs 'di su la'ang ma gnang bar: pra dun



gyi rgyal po spyan mi bzang gi mgul du sbas so: gcig bsam yas
chims phu be tsa gling gi mnam snang spyan la sbas pa rig
'dzin mnga' ris pan chen gyis gter nas gdan drangs pa'o:
gzhad pa rdo rje'i btsan pod kyi gros/
4) Gnod sbyin Tsitta dmar po'i gsol kha bzhugs
ff. 10r-llr
Incipit: Hri padma tsanda ma hā kro dha ha ya gr wa hu lu hu
lu hüm phat: mchod gtor legs par bshams la byin gyis brlabs
te rol pa skya bdun gyi las byang ni:

DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA RAB TU BYUNG BA'I CHA LUGS CAN
1. Thub pa Rdo rje gdan
2. Dam tshig gsum bkod lha lnga
3. Thub chen gnas brtan bcu drug gis bskor ba
4. Bka' gdams lha bzhi'i Thub pa chen po
5. Bcom idan 'das Sman bla
6. Sangs rgyas Klu dbang rgyal po
RNAL BYOR BLA MED
1. Gsang ba 'dus pa 'Jam pa'i rdo rje gtso rkyang
2. Mi bskyod rdo rje lhan skyes
3. Ma hā mā ya
4. 'Khor lo bde mchog lhan skyes

6. Go cha'i dpa' mo drug

8. Bde mchog dkar po'i Tshe sgrub

11. Dus 'khor lhan skyes
12. Khro rgyal Rdo rje shugs
13. Gshed dmar lhan skyes
14. Rdo rje 'jigs byed bsdus pa
RNAL BYOR MA'I PHYOGS
1. Nā ro mkha' spyod
2. Zhal gnyis ma Dpyal lugs
3. Mai tri mkha' spyod
4. Indra mkha' spyod

11. Phag mo Khros nag lha dgu
12. Phag dkar Shes rab gsal byed
SPYAN RAS GZIGS KYI SKOR

Author: Zhang-zhung-pa Blo-bzang-bstan-'dzin-rgyal-mtshan

na mo gu ru ma hā ka la ya/
Mye shes rang bzhin gar dgu'i 'jo sgeg can/
ha ha hūm gyi bzhad sgras sa gsum "dar/
srid gsum bdud bzhi'i khrag 'thung he ru ka/
che mchog khyod kyi bdag la thugs brtser mdzod
Zjigs dus zhugs ltar 'bar ba'i klong yangs na
kun tu thogs med gdug pa'i mtshon cha gd engs,
phrin las mam bzhi thogs med sgrub mdzad mgon/
dpal idan nag po chen po kun tu rgyal/
Akhyod nyid he ru ka pa'i ngo bo ru/
7gdod nas dag kyang tshur mthong snang ngo ru/
ye shes sgyu 'phrul kun khyab (f. 1v) mkha' dbyings la/
mam par rtsen pa'i sngon byung lo rgyus spel
de la 'dir dpal rdo rje nag po chen po phyag bzhi pa'i sngon
byung ba'i tshul ni/ sngon gyi dus su/ lha mnams dang/ lha ma yin
mams thabs shing g.yul bkye bas/ lha ma yin rnams bsad pa'i khrag
thig pa re la dmag mi mang po 'phel/ lha mams la de ltar mi 'phel
zhing nyams par gyur pas/ lha mams ni pham/ lha ma yin mams ni
rgyal bar gyur nas de'i tshe/ lha mams kyi dbang po brgya byin
gyis bcom ldan 'das la zhe sa dang bcas te gsol ba/
lha ma yin mams pham par gyur zhing/ lha mams rgyal bar
'gyur ba'i thabs ji ltar lags zhes zhus pa'i lan du/ ston pas/
dbang phyug chen po ri rab gyi khongs bseng na dka' thub
byed cing yod pa de Idog par gyis dang/ de'i bu mams kyis lha ma
yin gyi g.yul thams cad rmeg med (f. 2r) par 'joms par gyur rol
zhes gsungs/
de'i tshe lha mnams kyis sprul pa'i lha mo u ma de wa khrid
nas ri rab gyi khongs bseng du iha chen po la phul bas/ de dka'
thub las log ste/ lha mo u ma dang 'dus pa la bu mthu chen brgyad
'byung ste/ de yang/
gzhon nu karti ka dang/ nan ti ka dang/ tsan te dang/ bha
ru gri dang/ ha nu ma tha dang/ ga na pa ti dang/ nag po chen po
la sogs pa brgyad yod pa la/ nag po chen po ni lha'i dmag dpon
byas te/ lha dang lha ma yin g.yui thabs pa'i tshe lha ma yin gyi
khrag mnams sa la bo ru ma bcug par thod par bcus te thungs pas/
lha ma yin gyi dmag rnams ma 'phel zhing/ lha ma yin gyi g.yul
pham par gyur ro/
7'o na nag po chen po 'di 'jig rten pa yin nam snyam na/
skyon med de/ Tai ltar de bzhin gshegs pa mams kyi sku gsung thugs
kyi rten gsum la/ sprul sku'i rten ni reya gar rdo rje gdan/ longs
sku'i rten ni phyi'i rgya mtsho chen po na shel sku ma ha bhe ba
zhes pa mam snang gangs chen mt sho'i sku shin tu che ba phyag
mnyam gzhag mdzad pa'i gru mo'i bar nas sdzing(sic!) chen po rnams
gro bad sku'i lte ba man chad chu nang du nub pa/ zla ba nya ba'i
dus la lha mams kyis khrus gsol nas sku la bya brun sogs 'gos pa
thams cad byi dor byed pa sogs ngo mtshar dpag tu med cing/ jo bo
rje lha goig dpal mar me mdzad kyis gser gling la gshegs dus yang

1
gzigs par gsungs pa de yin/ chos sku'i rten ni chos dbyings kyi

rgya gar rdo rje gdan gyi shar lho o ta'i yul gyi bye brag na
kha sarpa ni rang byung gi gtsug lag khang bzhugs/ de nas zla ba

blo gros dang ldan pa rnams kyis thar pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa
sgrub pa'i grogs su chos skyong khyad par can 'di dag brten par
mdzod cig/
Zair smras pa/ he ru ka pa'i ye shes 'phrul bsgyur las/
mi sdug gar dgu'i rol mdzad ye shes mgon/
angos grub phrin las mam bzhi'i ba ng mdzod mchog/
skal idan skye boli don du thub pas rtsal/
blo bzang klu sgrub rnam dpyod ka randar/
mgon de'i man ngag zab mo'i zil mngar gtams/
stobs bcu mnga' ba'i bstan la lhag par du/
Zbya ba mdzad pa'i 'phrin las sgrubs 'dir ítos/
de las brgyud pa'i zab mo gnad kyi don/
dpal ldan rgwa lo'i thugs su 'khyil ba yis/,
bod yul rmongs pa'i dri ma kun 'khrud cing/
skal idan yongs la bka' drin mdzad 'dir mtshar/
7mchog mthun dngos grub tshul 'dir stsol mdzad cing/
Imthu stobs bskal pa'i me chen mched 'dra ba'i/
nag phyogs 'joms mdzad dpal ldan phyag bzhi par/
byang chub grogs su blo idan mams brten rigs/
Zphags yul dbus gyur na lenda yi grwa/
bod yul yilthig ler 'phos pa bzhin/
Mapal ldan bkra shis lhun po'i chos kyi grwar
dpal mgon lo rgyus gung sgrig bdag gi sbyar,
/ces bcom idan 'das nag po chen po phyag bzhi pa'i sngon byung gi
lo rgyus mgon po'i thugs mnyes par byed pa'i tshig gi mchod sprin
zhes bya ba 'di ni/ mnga' ris zhang zhung gi sa'i cha spe ti rang
rig (f. 8r) pa stag mo dge rgan drung ram pa dge slong blo bzang
bsam 'grub dang mnga' ris zangs mkhar ba bkal bcu blo bzang yar
'phel gnyis kyis 'di Ita bu zhig dgos zhes don gnyer chen pos
bskul ba'i ngor 7 rig sngags 'chang ba'i dge slong zhang zhung
pa 7 blo bzang bstan 'dzin rgyal mtshan gyis sbyar ba'o7 /mangga

Incipit:
Ina mo lo ke shwa ra ya:
bcu gsum rdo rje dzin pa'i sa chen thob pa:
bde bar gshegs pa'i zhing mchog dam pa 'di:
abyer med sbas yul 'bras ljongs kun gyi mchog gyur ba:
'phags mchog, (f. 1v) spyan ras szigs kyi zhing mchog Iha yi
dbang po brgya byin dang: rje btsun phags ma sgrol mas lung
bstan: pad byung lan brgyar mnga' gsol mdzad pa'i zhing mchog
dam pa: thog mar rgyal ba gnyis pa orgyan gyi slob dpon chen
po nyid: lho nub srin yul du byon nye tsam gyi dus: sngon tshe
ias smon mthu (f. 2r) las grub pa'i: 'bras ljongs hüm ra'i gdung
'dzin du byon rgyu'i: yab rig 'dzin mthong mchog mthong grol gyi
sras phyi ltar rdzi bo'i mtshan can: nang ltar gsang sngags
snying ma'i bla ma: yi dam thugs rje chen po'i ijags bsnyen la dus
rtag tu brtsun pa zhig yod pa de: g.yag lug gcig lcogs kyi rdzi
bor phebs te lo ngo gsum tsam gyi ring ljags bsnyen kho na mdzad
cing: g.yag lug mnams nyin mo zas khar so sor (f. 2v) rang ngo
thon pa dang: dgong mo rjes 'ded med par rang log gis yong ba sogs:
ya mtshan gyi mdzad pa star chags su yod pa las: zla ba dang

tsher

ba sems can raams sgrib pa sbyong ba'i phyir: khyed rang bzhugs

bas; nga dang dbyer med rgyal gar bsil ba tshal gyi dur khrod
du ba ru khru gang la nga yi rang byon yod pa de khyod la ster
byu
gsungs: mchod rten bzhengs ste bum ider longs pa dang: gong du
gsungs pa'i byu ru'i rta ngrin rang byon de nam mkha' nas thugs
gzungs su phebs pa dang: *mchod rten grub nas rab gnas skabs rta *(1. 3v)
skad lan gsum du 'tsher zhing: bskal ldan las 'phro can mchin
na snyigs dus kyang rta skad 'tsher ba yod: ces gsungs shing:
mtshan yang rta ngrin zhi ba'i mchod rten du grags shing:
gzhan yang rta mchog gis lung bstan bka' stsal pa: o rgyan chen
po lho nub tu phebs pa'i dus nye bar yod do: khyod kyang gsol ba
yang yang thob: ces gsungs so:
de nas sa ga zla ba'i tshes bcu nyin phyi ltar na glang phu
rtse Inga: nang ltar na bsam yas dpel icog rgyal (f. 4r) chen sku
Inga: gsang ba itar na gangs chen mdzod Inga'i gzungs g.yag zhol
po zhig yod pa de: thugs tshub che bar rdzi bo yang thugs rgyal
ita bu'i phyag 'khar lan gsum bkyon pas: zhol po de yang thugs
phams te gangs ri'i ljongs su byon pa dang mnyam du g.yag lug
byings kyang 'ur bas: rdzi bo'i rjes 'ded phebs pa dang 'od zer chen
po zhig gzigs gnang du byung ba dang: g.yag lug mnams kyang blo dal
zhing lhing chags pa 'byung ba: bza' hor ma'i khri chen po zhig gi
steng du: orgyan chen po sku mdos mnyams pa'i g.yas su 71. 4v)
lha lcam man dha ra ba: g.yon du ye shes mtsho rgyal dang: mtha' 'khor
du rig 'dzin grub chen pho mo mkha' gro
b'i tshogs dang bcas pa: mngon

ma rin po che yul gang nas phebs: da gang du bzhugs don ci'i phyir



byon: zhes gsol bas: gu rus bka' stsal pa:
ho nga ni padma 'byung gnas yin srin po mnams 'dul ba'i
phyir lho nub phyogs su bzhud do: zhes bkal stsal pas: yang
rdzi bos dad gus drag pos sngon rgya gar mi tris phul bas inda
(f. 5r) ni la'i phyag phreng zhig dang: kai ru'i tog gcig yod pa
de mandal gyi rten du phul nas: di skad zhus so:
snga brgya'i mthar ma mi mnams tshe thung nad gdon rkyen
ngan mang: khyad par mi dge bcu dang mtshams med Inga: de dang

dang phyogs mtshans mnams su brag rir itas ji ltas ji ltar lags:

ces gsol bas:
gu rus gsung gtor mdzad pas (f. 5v) phyag phreng de 'thor
ba'i tshul gyis: de ma thag khri zhabs nas yan lag, brgyad ldan
gyi bdud rtsi'i chu mig rdol zhing gangga'i rgyun 'bab pa dang:
@ ma ho dus gsum sangs rgyas 'dus pa'i khri zhabs nas bdud rtsi'i
chu mig brgya rtsa mchis pa las: khrus byas nad gdon bar chad zhi
zhing btung bas las dang sgrib pa dag: khyad par mi dge bcu dang

mdzod ma lus krug byas pa'i 'di 'dra'i gangga'i chu rgyun yod mi
srid: gzhan yang rgyab phyogs kyi brag ri la rdo rje mam joms
kyi gzugs sku dang: dkyil 'khor gyi rang byon yod:
dbus ri gza' rā hu la'i stan gzhi'i gnas ri: de'i rgyab

rdzi bo'i gdung dzin gyis zhal phye ba' i lung zin: 'dir zhib
rgyas ma spros so:
de nas shar phyogs su rgyangs grags kyi sa na byams pa
gdan bzhugs kyi brag rir chos sgo brgyad khri bzhi stong don bsdus

de'i (f. 7r) mdun na mtsho yod pa de la ltas na sems can so
so'i las dang sgrib pa spyi yang gi dbang las phyis byung skyes

'di nas byang ngos khro bo'i rgyal po kun tu bzang po che
mchog he ru ka: yab yum stong nyid thabs shes mdzad pa'i zhabs
'og tu: lan cig 'dzul na ngan song gsum gyi sdig sgrib dag: gzhan
yang rgyangs grags goig bgrod pa'i byang shar mtshams su: rgya
gar dur khrod bsil ba tshal am langka brtsigs pa dang ntshungs
pa'i dur khrod phyi nang gsang, gsum yod pa las: gsang ba'i dur
khrod na mkha' gro nyer lnga'i sprul pa rgya bskyed pa dang:
mi lpags g.yang bzhi la sogs pa rdo la rang byon du yod do:
(f. 8)
gnas 'dir mi rodgod khar bzhag kyang snga gro khyi spyang
dang, mkha' 1ding gis bzos grub bo: tshe 'das de yang yul nyer bzhi'i
mkha' gro'i gnas dang mtho ris sụ skye ba'i zhal bzhes: 'di nas
nub byang ngos rgyang grags gcig 'das pa'i sa na: gad sa zhal zas
dra ba'i rang byon ni rgyal ba sras bcas mnyes pa'i 'dod yon
sna lnga'i mchod sprin no:
rgyal ba'i zhing mchog rang byon mchod rten mam gsum gyi lo
brgyud ni: mtsho rgyal dang rdzi bo gnyis kyis tshogs mchod rgya
cher phul te: 'di skad (f. 9r) ces zhuso:
gnas 'di'i mtshan ji ltar lags gnas mjal phyag bskor byas
pa phan yon ji ltar yod: gu ru dus gsum khyen pas gab skyil med par
gsung du gsol: zhes zhus pas:
orgyan chen pos bka' stsal: khyod gnyis kyi blor gang shar
ba'i mchod rten re re dang mthun mong du gcig bzhengs dang: de'i
gzungs bzhugs tu shel khru gang la 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs rang
byon khrungs pa zhig g.yu lo bkod pa'i zhing mchog nas spyan
drangs la: de la bsu ba dang ser sbreng mchod pa sogs 'gyis shig
gsungs:
yang rdzi bos (f. 9v) 'di skad ces zhus: bdag la bu slob pho
mo sogs gcig kyang med pas ji ltar drag zhus pas:
gu rus bka' stsal pa: yid sprul gyi mchod pa dpag med phul:
zhes gsungs so:
de dus rdzi bos dad gus drag pos g.Jas su pho rgyud dang:
g.yon du mo rgyud bcas bran du bkul nas mdun du 'dod yon sna Inga'i
mchod pa dpag med phul gsungs pas: de'i skabs nyi ma shar tsam
du rdzi bos gzigs snang du shar phyogs kyi nam mkhar gser gyi
rdo rje rtse inga pa zhig gyur ba: dga' spro .dpag med mdzad pa
dang mnyam nyi ma shar ba (f. 10r) dang shel gyi mchod rten gong
du gsungs pa ji bzhin nam mkha' nas byon: gzungs su gzhugs nas mtsho
rgyal dang rdzi bo mthun mong du zheng ba: rang byon shel gyi mchod
rten 'di nyid dang: rdzi bo zheng pa rdzi bo'i mchod rten dang:
mtshọ rgyai bzheng ba 'brog mo mchod rten zhes bya ba: phyag gnas
mnga' gsol rgyas par mdzad skabs kyang me tog gi char babs cing:
mtshan ni rten 'brel gong gsal gyi dbang gis rdo rje nyi ma mchod
rten di mams la phyag bskor (f. 10v) mchod pa byas pa'i phan yon
ni: gong si chu mig 'di'i phan yon dang mtshungs shing: dge ba ci
byas 'bum?
gyur ngo mtshar brjod pa'i mtha' las 'das pa'o: sdig
pa bsags pa de bzhin no lhag par bud med bu 'dod pa la mchog tu
gyur ro: smon lam sna re btab na de nyid du thogs med 'grub bo:
zhes gsungs pa'i skabs su:
bod kha ba'i ljongs kyi gnas mchog nas: lho nub tu spyan dren
pa'i bsu ba ma dang mkha' gros bar snang gang bas: rje 'bangs
mams la zhal gdam mi (f. lir) grub pa'i thugs brel stabs kyi ngang:
yan lag brgyad ldan gyi mdun ngos rdo steng du zhabs rjes zhig byin
rlabs kyi rten du 'jog, gnang mdzad: zhal lho nub tu gzigs te ithi
sa ma ya rgya rgya: de'i dus kyi rdzi bo de ni sku goig la mtshan

gro'i
du mtshan gsol gnang zhing: byang phyogs jo bo gsung byon gyis
mtshan gsol ba grub chen nag po spyod pa mthu stobs zhes gsungs
pa: don du ngo bo dge slong nam mkha'i (f. llv) snying po sku
mngos te: dgung grangs kyang brgya tham pa bzhugs shing de la
sgo gsum syis, gsol ba btab na tshe sgrub brgya res byin mthu'o:
mthar sku ja' lus grub ste bde ba can gyi zhing du mkha'
tshogs dpon mdzad: thugs mchod rten mam gsum dang 'dra sku'i
snang brnyan la zhugs pa: gsung bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i don du
skye ba'i 'phreng ba la byon pa sogs zhal gyis bzhes pa'o:
de yang rang 'byung mchod rten rnam gsum la mkha' 'gro'i
bskor ba byed pa yin: mi ma yin gyis mchod dbyangs (f. 12r) phul
ba'o: gter kha dga' ri'i brag nas bzhes pa'i gnas yig ltar gsal:
gzhan dag na 'ongs lung bstan sogs rgya cher gsungs pa'i ma dpe
sbas yul 'bras mo ljongs su gsang ba'i gnas yig tu bka' gsal:
gnas kyi lte ba brag dkar bkra shis sding: shar phyogs sbas phug
ma mo mkha' gro sprin ltar 'dus pa mkha' gro gsang ba'i phug pa:
'chi med tshe ltar sgrub pa nub bde chen phug: mdzod Inga yi gter
kha mang du phye rgyu'i byang ina ri rin chen snying gi phug pa:
de'i mtshams brgyad kyi gnas gsang sngags (f. 12v) chos gling:
padma g.yang rtse: rab ldan rtse mo: mal 'byor che bzhi'i bsten
pa'i gzhi ma yug bsam thang dang nur gang mchod rten: ljon shing
royal po tsan dan gi ri rgyal: bar gyi gzhi bdag dpa' bo hüm ri
dang: phag mo rong dang khrag 'thung rong: rdo rje 'phreng dang
lcag sgrog 'phreng: mtsho chen brgya dang dgu la sogs: de yi bka'
'khor gangs chen mdzod lngas abus: gangs phran brgya dang, stong
phrag gcig sbas yul lho nag po bcas pa'i: rdo rje nyi ma di ni
sbas yul bras ljongs (f. 13r) kun gyi byang sgo'i sgo mchod yin
pa'i phyir ro:
chos bdag phyi nang gsang gsum dang: gza' mchog ra hu la dang:
'bar ba spun bdun jo mo tshe ring ma bcas la dbang ngo:
'gro don nyi zla ltar spyod par 'gyur ro: sa ma ya rgya rgya:
guru'i bka' bzhin mtsho rgyal gyi yi gir btab nas gter du sbas
phyi gter rdzi bo'i gsung, sprul edung rig 'dzin tshe dbang
egnyis pas: hüm ri brag sengge 'dra ba'i g.yas zur nas spyan drangs
pas: zhing khams mthing shog la tshal gyi brda' yig su bris 'dug
zhes: smon lam las 'phro rten 'brel 'azom pa'i (f. 13v) dus
mtshams su: bka' babs lung gzin rig. 'dzin rgod kyi ldem 'phru can:
lho bod mtshams kyi rdo rje nyi ma'i byang sgo brgyud nas bras
ljongs gnas sgo zhal phye skabs su: brda yig rams bod yig tu
to bka' phab mdzad te dbang skur man ngag zabs par gang te: ster

Buddhism in India

snyan pa'i sgra dbyangs.

sde tshan dang po'i dang po dbyangs yig dang pos brgyan pa/
bdun pa'i bzhi pa cung Zad na la zhon pa'i ming can rmal 'byor
dbang po skyes buli mchog gcig po 'dis ral gri la sogs pa'i
dngos grub chen po brgyad thob par 'gyur ro/
/de'i slob ma mnal 'byor pa drug gis lus kyi dngos po
spangs pa'i phyag rgya chen po thob par 'gyuro/ ces gsungs pa
dang/ DPAL DUS KYI 'KHOR LO'I RGYUD PHYI MA 'GYUR RNYING las/
kha twām ga dang rus rgyan cang te chang snod thogs pa
NAG PO'i ming can 'byung bar 'gyur/
/ces lung bstan pa ste/
lung dang po'i don ni der ces pas gang du (f. 2r) 'khrungs
pa'i yul dang/ brtson 'grus dang ldan zhing sbyor ba la brtson
pa ni/ rig pa brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa rgya cher spyod pa'i
don dang/ rā ma na'i bka'i 'jug pa dang mthun pa ni lang ka'i
gling la sogs par gdug pa can mams tshar gcod pa'i don dang/
sde tshan dang po'i dang po ka yig/ bdun pa'i bzhi pa ha yig/
cung Zad na la zhon pa ni ha yig de nyid na yig dang brtsegs pa
ste/ de Itar na KAHNA zhes pa mtshan bstan pa yin no/
/nag po'i skad dod mang du yod kyang/ kahna zhes pa slob
dpon 'di'i thun mongs ma yin pa'i mtshan te/ kannā tsarya'am/
'phral skad du/ kahni pa ces grag go/
/ral gri la sogs pa'i dngos grub brgyad ces pas/ thun
mong gi grab pa brgyad la mnga' brnyes pa ste gzhan la sbyin
nus pa'o/

Zrgyal ba yab sras gsum la gus phyag Ytshalſ
Akyai lags/ thabs mkhas thugs rje shākya'i rigs khrungs zhing/
Zgzhan gyi mi thub bsdud kyi dpung, 'joms pa/
Zgser syi lhun po lta bur brjid pa'i sku/
shākya'i rgyal po'i zhabs la gus phyag 'tshal/
stong nyid rtogs pa'i srid pa'i rgya mtsho bar/
snying rje dman pa zhi ba'i lam las 'das/
/bdag med don gyi 'byor la dbang bsgyur ba'i/
%' phags mchog dge 'dun gus pas rgya mtsho bdud/
phyi snod 'jig rten rgya gram rlung gi btag/
nang bcud sems can 'od gsal lha na s chad
Zgling gi mchog gyur lho'i 'dzam bu gling,
dgra bcom bzhugs gnas gti se gangs kyi gu
ma gros bzhugs gnas ma spang g.yu yi mtsho,
seng ge kha 'babs 'brug pa'i g.yas phyogs dir/
dam chos chos la dkar ba spyi ti chos yul
sa la 'bur tho rgyal sa brang khar rtser,
rdzong dpon chen po ga ga bskal bzang yab sras
dbur rmog tho zhing chab srid dar ba'i dus/

ågon pa khyad du 'phags pa nor bu dge 'phel nas/
đpon slob (f. lr) chen po blo bzang 'jam dbyangs chos btsug mthos
pas dus
khyed kyi chos bskor bzang po mnga' 'og tu/
yui la g.yang chags kyid pa'i g.yang yul lho shar 'dir/
phu ru rtsa chu 'jom zhing mdo ru 'bru sna min/
mi rigs khungs btsun rus chen rus pa'i rgyud/
dad ldan yon gyi bdag po blo bzang tshe ring dang/
tshe 'di 'gal rkyen bar chad zhi phyir dang/

sa dang/ no mo cu ngun dang/ tshama'i mchog gyur cu dun dang/

/chos mgon chen po nor bu dge 'phel nas mai dge slong nor bu'i
sol ja gung tshigs/ dge slong sam grub ma bu gnyis kyi gsol ja
gung tshigs chang tshos/ dbon po rdo rje tshe ring chang tshos/
tsho byed so nam rgyal po chang tshos gung tshigs), cur dpon bkra
shis rig 'dzin chang tshos nyin khang gung tshigs/ mai dgos pa
chang tshos/ dar rgyas gung tshigs sol ja/ mai 'bel tshe ring chang
tshos/ tshing so nam cang tshos/ tshing ti 'dzin chang tshos7 mai
grong 'der sol ja/ tshe ring 'bi krug chang tshos/ ngu 'brub sol
ja gung tshings/phun tshogs dar rgyas sol ja gung tshigs/ kyis
nas rig 'dzin dpal 'byor chang tshos nyin kyang yang yang/ no sri
lug chang tshos nyin khang/ khu rig nas dpai 'byor 'grong sum gyi
chang tshos nyin khang/ chang tshos (f. 1r) si kyin nas tin ngu
'brub chang tshos nyin khang/ a bi shes 'dzom dge'u, kyo mo na dkon
mchog age'u, dpal byor dge u/ mai sam grags pa dge'u/ a bi blo

On the rosary
Bla ma dgongs pa 'dus pa las: Phreng ba'i de nyid gsal ba
sngags kyi sgron me. From volume 3 (Ga) of an eastern Tibetan
print of the Bla ma dgongs 'dus collection.
na mo ghu ru dhe wa dā kki ni hūm:
byin rlabs ster 'byung bla ma rje:
dngos grub 'byung gnas yi dam lha:
phrin las mnga' bdag mkha' 'gro'i tshogs:
rtsa ba gsum la phyag 'tshal lo:
gsang sngags lam zhugs 'dod pa yis:
sngags kyi dkyil 'khor nyer brtson zhing:
sgrub pa mtha ru dbyung don du:
phreng ba'i de nyid gsal bar dkod:
de yang phreng ba'i ngo bo dang:
nges tshig de bzhin dbye ba dang:
rnam grangs dgos ched dam tshig ste:
de ltar drug gis stan la dbab:
dang po phreng ba'i ngo bo ni:
rtsar (f. lv) la brgyus dang grangs can dang:
rgyan du byas dang khrigs la 'bebs:
tshod 'dzin bsnyen pa'i slad du ste:
de sogs phreng ba'i ngo bor bshad:
gnyis pa phreng ba'i nges tshig ni:
dad dang ldan pa'i skyes mchog rnams:
bla ma la ni sems phreng bas:
gsol ba phur tshugs gdab pa dang:
sgrub pa nan tan byed 'dod pas:
yi dam lha la sems phreng zhing:
bsnyen pa tshul bzhin brtson pa dang:
phrin las dmigs su bsgyur 'dod pas:
mkha gro la ni sems phreng zhing:
las rnams mtha' ru dbyung ba ste: (f. 2r)
bla ma la ni sems phreng bas:
gdung ba drag po bskyed pa yis:
bla mas bdag la thugs phreng nas:
brtse ba chen pos byin gyis rlob:
yi dam lha la sems phreng bas:
sgrub la nan tan bskyed pa yis:
lha yis bdag la thugs phreng nas:
mehog dang thun mong ngos grub sbyên:
dā kki'i tshogs la sems phreng zhing:
phrin las drag tu bskul pa yis:
dā kkis bdag la thugs phreng bas:
ci 'dod phrin las sgrub par byed:
de bzhin mched dang lcam dral dang:
rdo rje spun grogs la sogs rnams:
phan tshun gcig la geig phreng bas:
dam tshig mams la mi 'da' zhing:
dkyil 'khor gcig tu bsgrub pa dang:
rdo rje srad bus sbrel ba yis:
dgongs pa gcig tu gyur pa rnams:
gcig sems gcig la phreng ba'o:
gsum pa phreng ba'i dbye ba ni:
mang du bshad kyang mdor bsdus pas:
zhi ba'i las la bsngags pa yi:
phreng ba de bzhin rgyas pa dang:
dbang gi las dang drag po'i las:



On the rosary: Sangs-rgvas-gling-pa
2
bskrad dang dgye (or: dbye) ba gtor ba'i las:
bshig pa'i las dang sna tshogs pa'i:
de dag mnams la bsngags pa yi: (f. 2v)
phreng ba mnams te de las gzhan:
phyi dang nang dang gsang, ba dang:
kho na nyid kyi phreng ba'o:
bzhi pa phreng ba'i rnam grangs ni:
dang du blang dang spang bya'o:
dang po dang du blang pa yi:
phreng ba'i rnam grangs 'di ltar ro:
rgyu dang kha dog che chung dang:
grangs dang de bzhin phreng thag dang:
mdo dzin dang ni bgrang tshul lo:
gyu ni rab la rin po che:
'bring ni shing gi bras bu ste:
tha mas shing dang sa rdo dang:
sman gyi 'de gu'i phreng ba'o:
dung ni zhi ba'i phreng ba ste:
zhi ba'i las kyi sngags la'o:
gser syi phreng ba rgyas pa'i las:
bye ru'i phreng ba dbang las grub:
lcags dang g.yu phreng drag po'i las:
gzi mchong sna tshogs las la shis:
sa la'i shing 'bras zhi ba'i las:
the'u kham 'bras rgyas pa 'grub:
lang thang dbang gi las la shis:
na ga khyung mchu rag sha yi:
drag po'i las kyi phreng bar bsngags:
bo dhi tsi ni kun la shis:
byang chub shing dang skya mnyen phreng:
zhi ba'i las kyi phreng bar shis:
To se la sogs bras bu can:
rgyas pa'i las sgrub phreng ba'o:
mdzo mo shing dang 'om bu'i phreng:
dbang gi las grub phreng bar (f. 3r) bsngags:
seng lding tsher nag drag po'i shing:
par slo shing gi phreng ba ni:
las rnams kun la bsngags pa'o:
sa ril zhi ba'i phreng ba las:
rdo yi phreng ba rgyas par shis:
sman gyi phreng ba dbang las 'grub:
thod pa la sogs rus chen gyi:
phreng ba drag po'i las 'grub 'gyur:
sna tshogs bsdus pa'i phreng bas ni:
las rnams thams cad 'grub ces bshad:
kha dog dag kyang 'di Ita ste:
dkar po zhi ba'i las la bsngags:
kha dog ser po rgyas pa'i phreng:
dbang la kha dog dmar po'i phreng:
nag po drag po'i phreng bar bsngags:
las rnams kun la khra bor bshad:
gzhan yang shing phreng zhi ba la:
rin po che yi phreng ba rnams :
rgyas pa'i las 'grub phreng ba ste:
shing 'bras phreng ba dbang las 'grub:
drag po rus chen phreng ba'o:
bskrad dang dbye dang gtor ba dang:

On the rosary: Sangs-rgyas-gling-pa
3
bshig pa la sogs phreng ba ni:
gzhan nas 'byung gi 'dir ma smos:
ba so phreng bas las rnams 'grub:
mdzes pa'i mam par byas pa yi:
phreng ba rgyan du byas pa ni:
lung ma bstan gyi phreng ba'o:
che chung tshad ni 'di Ita ste:
zhi ba rang gi 'gram so'i tshad: (f. 3v)
rgyas pa la ni mthe bong tsam:
dbang phreng nor bu'i tog dang mnyam:
drag po'i phreng ba rkang pa yi:
theb chen tshad dang mnyam pa ste:
'on kyang nor bu'i phreng ba dang:
shing 'bras rang rang tshad kyis bzung:
rang dod la ni nges med brtan:
bzos pa'i rigs la gong bzhin no:
nges med lung ma bstan gyi rigs:
nus pa mi 'byin spang bar bya:
phreng ba'i grangs kyi tshad bstan pa:
spyi la brgya dang brgyad bsngags kyang:
yang na de phyed Inga bcu bzhi:
nyer bdun dang ni bcu bzhi ste:
zhi ba'i las sngags gang 'dren yang:
bcu gcig grangs tshad yang yang bskyal:
brgya stong khri 'bum la sogs pa:
bsnyen grangs tshad bzung gzhung dang bstun:
de bzhin rgyas pa brgya rtsa brgyad:
dbang la lnga bcu rtsa bzhi'i grangs:
drag po la ni nyer gcig go:
kun kyang rang rang gzhung lugs ltar:
grangs kyi bsnyen pa tshad du bskyal:
de ltar mam pa bzhi dag las:
mang bar mi bya nyung mi bya:
phreng ba'i rgyun thag 'di ita ste:
zhi ba bal skud dkar po la:
rgyas par ras skud ser pos sbrel:
dbang phreng dar skud dmar pos sbrel:
drag po'i (f. 4r) phreng ba gri rgyus sam:
yang na rgyus chen sbrel bar bya:
de bzhin rgyu ma lpags pa'i rigs:
rgyun bu gras pa'i rigs kyis sbrel:
sna tshogs las kyi phreng thag ni:
tshon skud lnga sgril srad bu ste:
kun kyang phra sbom phreng ba yi:
mig dang bstun la ran par bya:
yangs pa ma yin dogs pa min:
ring ba ma yin thung ba min:
ha cang dogs na las mi 'grub:
yangs na gseb 'tshang bar chad 'jug:
ring na lha 'gyang bsgrub pa g.yel:
ha cang thung na tshe la gzan:
mdud pa can dang mdud pa chags:
phra sbom ma snyoms go dka'ang 'byung:
de sogs ram dbye shes par bya:
phreng ba'i mdo 'dzin 'di ltar bya:
zhi ba akar zhing zlum la 'gril:
rgyas pa ser po rgya mdud can:
yang na lcim gzhog mchod rten ris:



On the rosary: Sangs-rgyas-gling-pa
4
dbang la kha dog dmar po dang:
dbyibs ni leb dang zla gam dang:
nar mo nyid kyang shis pa'o:
drag po kha dog nag po'i cha:

zur can bug pa tshag tshag can:

mdo 'dzin sku gsung, thugs kyi rgya:

ye shes spyan drangs bug cing bstim:
lag pa g.yas pas me tog la:
lha sngags rten 'brel snying po dang:
a li ka li bzlas pas gtor:
khyad par sngags grangs brgya rtsa brgyad :
om ru tsi pra ma dha na ye ratna mā le dha ra dznyā na dhe wa
a bhi şi nytsa hüm swā hã: zhes sogs sngags kyi yig 'bru mams:
gang byed las kyi kha dog can:
dkar ser dmar 1jang char bzhin 'bebs:

gnyis med gcig tu gyur nas kyang:
sku gsung thugs kyi rang bzhin can:
od du zhu ba'i phreng bar dmigs:
shis pa brjod cing las la sbyar:
thog mar 'bru gsum brgya rtsa bzla:
de nas a li ka li dang:
rten 'brel snying po phreng ba'i sngags:
nyer (f. 5r) gcig la sogs ci 'grub bzla:
de nas gang yin bzlas pa 'bad:
de ltar idan pa'i phreng ba de:
phal pa mnams dang mi 'dra bas:

5
'gug pa'i 'dun pas bsgrang bar bya:

yang na dam tshig gcig nges pa'i:

"bras bu mi zad spel phyir dang:

On the rosary: Sangs-rgyas-gling-pa
6.
bye brag sngags kyi grangs tshad 'dzin:
de yang gsang sngags rig sngags dang:
gzungs sngags la sogs sngags kyi rigs:
mthar thug bsgrang bar byed pa las:
tshad mams 'dzin pa'i slad du ste:
grangs tshad phreng ba las byung phyir:

List A
This list mentions the collections, canonical and non-canonical,
preserved at the monastery of Thyangpoche. None of these collections
are especially rare,
1. Kanjur
Rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che snar than par ma
(Tibetan Buddhist canon; Narthang redaction)
Common; examples at a number of institutions throughout the
world.
2. Tanjur
Bstan 'gyur snar than par ma
(Commentaries, largely translated from Sanskrit, on scriptures
found in the Kanjur; Narthang redaction)
Common; examples available at a number of institutions throughout
the world.
3. Rñin ma'i rgyud 'bum
(Collection of the tantras accepted by the Nyingmapa sect but
largely rejected by other schools; Sde-dge (Derge) edition in
26 volumes)
Xylographic edition at ISMEO in Rome; manuscript set in the
India Office Library; at least five sets in India; now under
reprinting under the patronage of the Queen Mother of Bhutan.
The blocks for two volumes have already been carved.
4. Kon-sprul Blo-gros-mtha'-yas, 1813-1899, comp.
Rin chen gter mdzod
(Collection of texts concerned with the practices connected with
the revealed and rediscovered teachings of Tibetan Lamaism;
largely written by Kon-sprul to show the essential coherence
of this massive body of extra-canonical literature; Mtshur-phu
(Tshurpu) edition in 63 volumes)
Common; numerous examples in India and abroad.
5. Nag-dba-blo-þzan-rgya-mtsho, 5th Dalai Lama, 1617-1682.
Gor sa lra pa'i gsur rnam lha sa'i par ma
(Collected works of the 5th Dalai Lama; Lhasa edition in 21
volumes; this example is apparently missing four volume Bka'
rgya ma; or, "sealed volumes")
Relatively common; many examples in the Soviet Union, Mongolia,
6. Kion-chen-pa Dri-ned-od-zer, 1308-1363.
Klor chen md zod bdun sgrags yan rdzon par ma
(The summa of Nyingmapa thought; four large volumes in this
Central Tibetan xylographic edition)
Common; the whole collection has recently been reprinted by
Dodrup Chen Rimpoche from Gangtok. This edition based on the
more reliable Khampa editions is excellent.
7. Sñin thig ya bãi.
Zab mo yan thig pod goig sgrags yar rdzor spar ma
(A portion of the most important Nyingmapa Atiyoga collection)
Common; now being reprinted in India.
8. Sõin thig ya bãi.
Bla ma yar thig
(Portion of the most important Nyingmapa Atiyoga collection)
Common; now being reprinted in India.
9. Sõin thig ya bãi.
Mkha' 'gro yan thig
(Portion of the most important Nyingmapa Atiyoga collection)
Now being reprinted in India.



List 1
WORKS ON MADHYAMIKA PHILOSOPHY
1. Ror-ston Ses-bya-kun-rig, 1367-1449.
Dbu ma rtsa ba'i mam bsad
(Exegesis of Nāgärjuna's Mūlamadhyamakakārikās from the Sa-
skya-pa approach)
Rare; probably the Sde-dge or Nalendra edition.
02. Ron-ston Ses-bya-kun-ris, 1367-1449.
Ses spriris mam bśad
(Exegesis of Nāgārjuna's Suhrllekha)
Rare; probably the Sde-dge or Nalendra edition.
3. Go-rams-pa Bsod-nams--sen-ge, 1429-1489.
Dbu ma'i spyi don nes don rab gsal
(Sa-skya-pa exegesis of Madhyamika)
Common; included in the Japanese reprint of the Sa skya bka'
'bum
4. Go-rams-pa Bsod-nams-ser-ge, 1429-1489.
Dbu ma'i dka! grel lta ba nan sel
(Difficulties in the proper understanding of Madhyamika philo-
sophy explained; a Sa-skya-pa commentary)
Common; included in the Japanese reprint of the Sa skya bka'
'bum.
15. Ratna-árī-bhadra.

(Exegesis of Dandin's Kävyadārsa)
Rare.
3. U-rgyan-bstan-'dzin, 'Bras-ljors-pa.
Sñan nag don rgyan so l'a'i dper brjod sñin po bsdus pa blo gsar
bun ba rol pa'i dga' tshal 'bras ljors pa o rgyan kun bzan
(Examples of the thirty five varieties of poetical adornments
described in the second chapter of Dandin's Kavyadāría)
Common; once reprinted in India since 1959.
4. U-rgyan-bstan-'dzin, 'Bras-ljons-pa.
Dbyans can nag gi rol mtsho las don rgyan so l'a'i sñin po bsdus
pa blo gsar buri ba rol pa orgyan kun bzar bstan 'dzin
7Second portion of the author's commentary on Dandin's Kävyadārsa)
Common; many examples of the Phun-khan print are available.
5. Dandin, 7th cent.
Sñan rag me lon ma'i rtsa ba/ slob dpon dbyug pa can
(Tibetan translation of the Kävyadārša)
Common; several reprints in India since 1959.
6. Tsoi-kha-pa Blo-bzar-grags-pa, 1357-1419.
Rtag tu ru'i rtogs brjod sñan drags dpag bsam gyi ljon pa
(Poetical rendering of the story of the Bodhisattva Sadāprarudita)
Common; once reprinted in India since 1959.

ye brdzu zhes pa'i sgrub thabs yig mying gi 'khrug gsal re
khyad par bkod pa bzhugs so
dgra bla chen po ye brdzu rdo rje bdud 'dul gyi mchod phrin kha skong
'dod 'jo'i bum bzang dge legs phreng mdzes
karma don grub dpal ldan bsod nams dbang phyug tshe
ring rnam par rgyal ba'i sde
ye brdzu'i dgra chos shin du gnyan pa'i bka' rgya gzhan la mi
spel dam tshig
dgra lha rke rgyal wer shod sngon po'i bsangs mchod 'dod dgu
'ching ba'i zhag pa mdo khams pa las rab bde chen rtsal
mgon po ye brdzu'i bskang mdos bkra shis rab 'bar
karma chags med
gnas bdag ye brdzu'i 'phrin bcol phrin las myur sgrub
rtogs ldan shakya shri
